	writefile_53();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '2a68c81ee621970777536474767268e7872bb3b2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '2a68c81ee621970777536474767268e7872bb3b2') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'fda6113594adbd92ceef86350973cd31d864ba0b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_53();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '2a68c81ee621970777536474767268e7872bb3b2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_56();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php') !== '987da4dc07736453f49ca6cf8aef9af00200350b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php');
		}
	}
}
